<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>How to use genepopedit</strong></h1><a id="user-content-how-to-use-genepopedit" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How to use genepopedit" href="#how-to-use-genepopedit"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Example data for the use in the following documentation is included within genepopedit.
The example genepop data is a GenePop data format with 10 populations, 30 individuals per population, and 100 Loci.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#Load example data in your workspace. 'GenePopData' will now be available for use.
  data(&quot;genepopedit_data&quot;)
  head(GenePopData) #View the data and the first 4 loci names. "><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>Load example data in your workspace. 'GenePopData' will now be available for use.</span>
  data(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>genepopedit_data<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
  head(<span class="pl-smi">GenePopData</span>) <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>View the data and the first 4 loci names. </span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">If reading in data to your workspace use the following <em>read.table</em> code specifics and associated parameters (sep="\t",quote="",stringsAsFactors=FALSE)</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#Example file path to your data
  file.link &lt;- &quot;c:/Users/YOUR NAME/Documents/Data/genepopdata.txt&quot;

#If your dataset has fewer than ~15,000 loci *read.table* should suffice
  GenePop &lt;- read.table(file.link,sep=&quot;\t&quot;,quote=&quot;&quot;,stringsAsFactors=FALSE)

#If your dataset has a large amount of loci (&gt;15,000) then we suggest using the data.table package to load in the data more efficiently.
  GenePop &lt;- data.table::fread(file.link,header=FALSE, sep=&quot;\t&quot;,stringsAsFactors=FALSE)"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>Example file path to your data</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">file.link</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>c:/Users/YOUR NAME/Documents/Data/genepopdata.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>If your dataset has fewer than ~15,000 loci *read.table* should suffice</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">GenePop</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> read.table(<span class="pl-smi">file.link</span>,<span class="pl-v">sep</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-cce">\t</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-v">quote</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-v">stringsAsFactors</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-c1">FALSE</span>)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>If your dataset has a large amount of loci (&gt;15,000) then we suggest using the data.table package to load in the data more efficiently.</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">GenePop</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> <span class="pl-smi">data.table</span><span class="pl-k">::</span>fread(<span class="pl-smi">file.link</span>,<span class="pl-v">header</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-c1">FALSE</span>, <span class="pl-v">sep</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-cce">\t</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-v">stringsAsFactors</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-c1">FALSE</span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">However, reading in your GENEPOP data into the workspace is not required, as all functions can work with both workspace objects <em>and</em> <strong>file paths</strong>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Set a directory where the output files will be saved.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="output_dir &lt;- &quot;c:/Users/YourName/Documents/GenePopFiles/&quot; "><pre><span class="pl-smi">output_dir</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>c:/Users/YourName/Documents/GenePopFiles/<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> </pre></div>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Preparation</strong> <a name="user-content-genepopidfix"></a></h1><a id="user-content-preparation-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Preparation" href="#preparation-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">genepop_ID</h2><a id="user-content-genepop_id" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: genepop_ID" href="#genepop_id"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Functions available in <strong>genepopedit</strong> require that the population and sample number be separated by an _ in the sample ID (e.g. BON_01 not BON01). This can be accomplished manually using a text editor or using the function <strong>genepop_ID</strong>. genepop_ID will read in a Genepop file and look for a common character string within the sample ID vectors grouped by the Genepop "Pop" labels. This function assumes that there <em>is</em> a common string which unifies IDs between each of the Pop labels. If this isn't the case, some pre-filtering of the data using a text editor will be required. <a href="#funcmanip"><em>Function description</em></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#Use genepop_ID to fix the sample IDs prior to the use of genepopedit functions.
filepath=&quot;~myfile.txt&quot; #path to 'myfile' which has sample IDs without the required _ separation. Note this can also be an object in the workspace.

genepop_ID(genepop=filepath, path=paste0(output_dir,&quot;Genepop_SampleID_fixed.txt&quot;))"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>Use genepop_ID to fix the sample IDs prior to the use of genepopedit functions.</span>
<span class="pl-v">filepath</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>~myfile.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>path to 'myfile' which has sample IDs without the required _ separation. Note this can also be an object in the workspace.</span>

genepop_ID(<span class="pl-v">genepop</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-smi">filepath</span>, <span class="pl-v">path</span><span class="pl-k">=</span>paste0(<span class="pl-smi">output_dir</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Genepop_SampleID_fixed.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))</pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">genepop_detective</h2><a id="user-content-genepop_detective" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: genepop_detective" href="#genepop_detective"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This function queries meta-data from your genepop data without having to open it in a text editor. Function returns a vector of population names, population counts, sample IDs, or Loci names. <a href="#funcdiag"><em>Function description</em></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Return <em>population names</em></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="PopNames &lt;- genepop_detective(GenePopData, variable=&quot;Pops&quot;)"><pre><span class="pl-smi">PopNames</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> genepop_detective(<span class="pl-smi">GenePopData</span>, <span class="pl-v">variable</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Pops<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)</pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">genepop_allelefreq <a name="user-content-genepopafreq"></a></h2><a id="user-content-genepop_allelefreq-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: genepop_allelefreq " href="#genepop_allelefreq-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This function will calculate allele frequencies based on the major allele among populations for each population group. <a href="#funcdiag"><em>Function description</em></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#calculate major allele frequencies according to the default population groupings.
  AlleleFreq_default &lt;- genepop_allelefreq(GenePopData)

#calculate major allele frequencies according to the specified population groupings.
  popgrouping &lt;- data.frame(Name=c(&quot;AAA&quot;,&quot;BBB&quot;,&quot;CCC&quot;,&quot;DDD&quot;,&quot;EEE&quot;,&quot;FFF&quot;),groups=c(&quot;gr1&quot;,&quot;gr1&quot;,&quot;gr2&quot;,&quot;gr2&quot;,&quot;gr3&quot;,&quot;gr3&quot;))

  AlleleFreq_specified &lt;- genepop_allelefreq(GenePopData, popgroup=popgrouping)"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>calculate major allele frequencies according to the default population groupings.</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">AlleleFreq_default</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> genepop_allelefreq(<span class="pl-smi">GenePopData</span>)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>calculate major allele frequencies according to the specified population groupings.</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">popgrouping</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> <span class="pl-k">data.frame</span>(<span class="pl-v">Name</span><span class="pl-k">=</span>c(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>AAA<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>BBB<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>CCC<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>DDD<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>EEE<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>FFF<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),<span class="pl-v">groups</span><span class="pl-k">=</span>c(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>gr1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>gr1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>gr2<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>gr2<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>gr3<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>gr3<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))

  <span class="pl-smi">AlleleFreq_specified</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> genepop_allelefreq(<span class="pl-smi">GenePopData</span>, <span class="pl-v">popgroup</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-smi">popgrouping</span>)</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">genepop_filter_maf <a name="user-content-genepopmaf"></a></h2><a id="user-content-genepop_filter_maf-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: genepop_filter_maf " href="#genepop_filter_maf-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This function will calculate global minor allele frequencies and filter based on a user defined threshold. <a href="#funcdiag"><em>Function description</em></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#Filter loci with minor allele frequencies less than 0.07.
 genepop_filter_maf(genepop=&quot;genepopedit_examplefile.txt&quot;,where.plink=&quot;c:/Users/YOURNAME/Documents/Programs/plink/&quot;,where.pgdspider=&quot;c:/Users/YOURNAME/Documents/Programs/PGDSpider_2.0.9.0/&quot;,maf=0.07,path=paste0(output_dir,&quot;Genepop_maf_0-07.txt&quot;)) "><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>Filter loci with minor allele frequencies less than 0.07.</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">genepop_toploci <a name="user-content-genepoptoploc"></a></h2><a id="user-content-genepop_toploci-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: genepop_toploci " href="#genepop_toploci-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This function will calculate linkage disequilibrium and global Weir and Cockerham's Fst for loci among populations. The function seeks a loci panel which maximizes global Fst for unlinked loci. The returned object is a list containing Linked loci ($Linked), global FST ($FST) and the top unlinked loci by FST ($FST_Unlinked). Note 'linked' loci are calcuated based on the threshold R<sup>2</sup> of 0.2 used by PLINK. This threshold (0-1) can be adjusted, though values &lt;0.2 may be limited by computational resources. Note that the available RAM for conversions using PGDspider is limited to 1 GB on Windows based operating systems. For the time being, this function only works with <strong>Plink 1.9</strong>. Use of Plink 2.0 will create function issues. <a href="#funcdiag"><em>Function description</em></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Warning messages &amp; diagnostics will be returned to the console by PGDspider &amp; PLINK. These warnings are expected.</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="
#Evaluate Fst and linkage among all loci and return an unlinked panel optimized by global Fst. 
#To calculate LD we use PLINK which requires a file conversion using PGDspider. 

  TopLoci &lt;- genepop_toploci(genepop=&quot;genepopedit_examplefile.txt&quot;,
  where.plink=&quot;c:/Users/YOURNAME/Documents/Programs/plink/&quot;,
  where.pgdspider=&quot;c:/Users/YOURNAME/Documents/Programs/PGDSpider_2.0.9.0/&quot;,fst.threshold = 0.04)
  
#Linked loci
  TopLoci$Linked
  
#Loci FST among populations
  TopLoci$FST
  
#Maximized FST by unlinked loci
  TopLoci$FST_Unlinked
  "><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>Evaluate Fst and linkage among all loci and return an unlinked panel optimized by global Fst. </span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>To calculate LD we use PLINK which requires a file conversion using PGDspider. </span>

  <span class="pl-smi">TopLoci</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> genepop_toploci(<span class="pl-v">genepop</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>genepopedit_examplefile.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-v">where.plink</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>c:/Users/YOURNAME/Documents/Programs/plink/<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-v">where.pgdspider</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>c:/Users/YOURNAME/Documents/Programs/PGDSpider_2.0.9.0/<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-v">fst.threshold</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.04</span>)
  
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>Linked loci</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">TopLoci</span><span class="pl-k">$</span><span class="pl-smi">Linked</span>
  
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>Loci FST among populations</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">TopLoci</span><span class="pl-k">$</span><span class="pl-smi">FST</span>
  
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>Maximized FST by unlinked loci</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">TopLoci</span><span class="pl-k">$</span><span class="pl-smi">FST_Unlinked</span>
  </pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Manipulation</strong></h1><a id="user-content-manipulation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Manipulation" href="#manipulation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">subset_genepop <a name="user-content-subsetgenp"></a></h2><a id="user-content-subset_genepop-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: subset_genepop " href="#subset_genepop-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Create a new Genepop file which only contains Loci <em>3, 15, 23, 49, 62, 81, 88, &amp; 94</em>. This useful if, for example, you identify loci which are potentially under selection and want a parsed dataset. Here our loci are named in the Loci# (1:100). <a href="#funcmanip"><em>Function description</em></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#inspect the names of the loci within the Genepop data
  genepop_detective(GenePopData,&quot;Loci&quot;)

#subset the Genepop file and 'keep' the specified loci names.
  subloci &lt;-c(&quot;Loci03&quot;,&quot;Loci15&quot;,&quot;Loci23&quot;,&quot;Loci49&quot;,&quot;Loci62&quot;,&quot;Loci81&quot;,&quot;Loci88&quot;,&quot;Loci94&quot;)

<p dir="auto">You can also remove populations within this function. Here we again select loci under selection, but remove populations 3 &amp; 7 (CCC/GGG). To do this we create a list of all populations we want to keep
(e.g. AAA, BBB, CCC ... JJJ)</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#use genepop_detective to find the population names
  PopNames &lt;- genepop_detective(GenePopData,&quot;Pops&quot;)

#create a list of populations you want to keep
  #manual
  PopKeep &lt;- c(&quot;AAA&quot;,&quot;BBB&quot;,&quot;DDD&quot;,&quot;EEE&quot;,&quot;FFF&quot;,&quot;HHH&quot;,&quot;III&quot;,&quot;JJJ&quot;)
#or
  #if you have fewer pops to remove
  PopKeep &lt;- setdiff(PopNames, c(&quot;CCC&quot;,&quot;GGG&quot;))

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">subset_genepop_rename <a name="user-content-subsetrenm"></a></h2><a id="user-content-subset_genepop_rename-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: subset_genepop_rename " href="#subset_genepop_rename-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Now change the names of some of the populations. In this example we will rename populations DDD &amp; HHH to YYY &amp; ZZZ. <a href="#funcmanip"><em>Function description</em></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#view the population names
  genepop_detective(GenePopData,&quot;Pops&quot;)

#create a dataframe for renaming. 
#column 1 = the original pop names.
#column 2 = the new names. 
  PopRename &lt;- data.frame(oPop = c(&quot;AAA&quot;,&quot;BBB&quot;,&quot;CCC&quot;,&quot;DDD&quot;,&quot;EEE&quot;,&quot;FFF&quot;,&quot;GGG&quot;,&quot;HHH&quot;,&quot;III&quot;,&quot;JJJ&quot;),
  newname = c(&quot;AAA&quot;,&quot;BBB&quot;,&quot;CCC&quot;,&quot;YYY&quot;,&quot;EEE&quot;,&quot;FFF&quot;,&quot;GGG&quot;,&quot;ZZZ&quot;,&quot;III&quot;,&quot;JJJ&quot;))

#rename populations
  subset_genepop_rename(genepop= GenePopData, path = paste0(output_dir,&quot;Genepop_renamed.txt&quot;),nameframe = PopRename)"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>view the population names</span>
  genepop_detective(<span class="pl-smi">GenePopData</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Pops<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>create a dataframe for renaming. </span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>column 1 = the original pop names.</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>column 2 = the new names. </span>
  <span class="pl-smi">PopRename</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> <span class="pl-k">data.frame</span>(<span class="pl-v">oPop</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> c(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>AAA<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>BBB<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>CCC<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>DDD<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>EEE<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>FFF<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>GGG<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>HHH<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>III<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>JJJ<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
  <span class="pl-v">newname</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> c(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>AAA<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>BBB<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>CCC<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>YYY<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>EEE<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>FFF<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>GGG<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>ZZZ<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>III<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>JJJ<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>rename populations</span>
  subset_genepop_rename(<span class="pl-v">genepop</span><span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">GenePopData</span>, <span class="pl-v">path</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> paste0(<span class="pl-smi">output_dir</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Genepop_renamed.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),<span class="pl-v">nameframe</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">PopRename</span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Populations can also be grouped by a common name. The result is similar to subset-genepop-aggregate except that population names will be replaced. Here it is useful to enable renumbering (renumber = TRUE) or there individuals with the same number will be assigned the same ID, if populations are combined.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#view the population names
  genepop_detective(GenePopData,&quot;Pops&quot;)

#create a dataframe for renaming. 
#column 1 = the original pop names.
#column 2 = the new names. 
  PopRename_group &lt;- data.frame(oPop = c(&quot;AAA&quot;,&quot;BBB&quot;,&quot;CCC&quot;,&quot;DDD&quot;,&quot;EEE&quot;,&quot;FFF&quot;,&quot;GGG&quot;,&quot;HHH&quot;,&quot;III&quot;,&quot;JJJ&quot;),newname = c(&quot;Pop1&quot;,&quot;Pop1&quot;,&quot;Pop1&quot;,&quot;Pop1&quot;,&quot;Pop1&quot;,&quot;Pop2&quot;,&quot;Pop2&quot;,&quot;Pop2&quot;,&quot;Pop2&quot;,&quot;Pop2&quot;))

  subset_genepop_rename(genepop= GenePopData, nameframe = PopRename_group, renumber = TRUE, meta=&quot;Pop&quot;,path = paste0(output_dir,&quot;Genepop_renamed_renumbered.txt&quot;))"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>view the population names</span>

<p dir="auto">Alternatively the sampleIDs can be renamed directly.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#create a renaming vector (column 1 = old column 2 = new)

<p dir="auto">If your sample IDs are not split between the population and the sample number using an _ then you can rename the populations before using any subsetting functions. Note that in this example because there is already a _ separating populations the</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#view the sample IDs
PopNames &lt;- genepop_detective(GenePopData,&quot;Inds&quot;)
PopNames_fixed &lt;- paste0(PopNames,&quot;_&quot;) #add the underscore seperator

#create a dataframe for renaming. 
  PopRename_fixed &lt;- data.frame(oPop = PopNames, newname = PopNames_fixed)

#rename populations * note here you will keep the original sample #s (renumber = F)
  subset_genepop_rename(genepop= GenePopData, path = paste0(output_dir,&quot;Genepop_renamed_renumbered.txt&quot;),nameframe = PopRename_fixed, renumber = FALSE)"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>view the sample IDs</span>

<span class="pl-smi">PopNames_fixed</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> paste0(<span class="pl-smi">PopNames</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>_<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>) <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>add the underscore seperator</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>create a dataframe for renaming. </span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">subset_genepop_aggregate <a name="user-content-subsetagg"></a></h2><a id="user-content-subset_genepop_aggregate-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: subset_genepop_aggregate " href="#subset_genepop_aggregate-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Now lets change group some populations together. In this example we will combine populations DDD/EEE &amp; FFF/HHH and remove populations JJJ/GGG (<em>not listed in column 1 of PopRename</em>). No loci will be removed from this dataframe (<em>subs = NULL</em>). This is useful when you don't want a clustering program (e.g. STRUCTURE or Bayescan) to assume differences among population groups. <a href="#funcmanip"><em>Function description</em></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#Use genepop_detective to find the meta-data for populations
  genepop_detective(GenePopData,&quot;Pops&quot;)

#create a dataframe for renaming. 
#column 1 = the original pop names and the list of pops required.
#column 2 = Grouping variables. 
  PopAggregate &lt;-data.frame(oP = c(&quot;AAA&quot;,&quot;BBB&quot;,&quot;CCC&quot;,&quot;DDD&quot;,&quot;EEE&quot;,&quot;FFF&quot;,&quot;HHH&quot;,&quot;III&quot;),
  agname = c(&quot;AAA&quot;,&quot;Pop1&quot;,&quot;CCC&quot;,&quot;Pop1&quot;,&quot;DDD&quot;,&quot;Pop2&quot;,&quot;HHH&quot;,&quot;Pop2&quot;))

#re-cast Genepop format to group populations based on 'PopAggregate'
  subset_genepop_aggregate(genepop= GenePopData, subs = NULL, path = paste0(output_dir,&quot;Genepop_grouped.txt&quot;),agpopframe = PopAggregate)"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>Use genepop_detective to find the meta-data for populations</span>
  genepop_detective(<span class="pl-smi">GenePopData</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Pops<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>create a dataframe for renaming. </span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>column 1 = the original pop names and the list of pops required.</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>column 2 = Grouping variables. </span>
  <span class="pl-smi">PopAggregate</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span><span class="pl-k">data.frame</span>(<span class="pl-v">oP</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> c(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>AAA<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>BBB<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>CCC<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>DDD<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>EEE<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>FFF<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>HHH<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>III<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
  <span class="pl-v">agname</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> c(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>AAA<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Pop1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>CCC<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Pop1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>DDD<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Pop2<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>HHH<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Pop2<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))

<p dir="auto">Now that we have two grouped populations, we can use the population rename function to give them a common name.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#read in the grouped Genepop file
  GenePopData2 &lt;-read.table(paste0(output_dir,&quot;Genepop_grouped.txt&quot;),header = FALSE, sep = &quot;\t&quot;, quote = &quot;&quot;, stringsAsFactors = FALSE)

#investigate the population parameters
  genepop_detective(GenePopData2,&quot;Pops&quot;)

#we can see that &quot;BBB&quot; &amp; &quot;DDD&quot; and &quot;FFF&quot; &amp; &quot;III&quot; are at the end but still have different names. 

#create renaming frame
  PopRename &lt;- data.frame(oPop = c(&quot;AAA&quot;,&quot;CCC&quot;,&quot;EEE&quot;,&quot;HHH&quot;,&quot;BBB&quot;,&quot;DDD&quot;,&quot;FFF&quot;,&quot;III&quot;),
  newname = c(&quot;AAA&quot;,&quot;CCC&quot;,&quot;EEE&quot;,&quot;HHH&quot;,&quot;Group1&quot;,&quot;Group1&quot;,&quot;Group2&quot;,&quot;Group2&quot;))

#Rename the grouped populations
  subset_genepop_rename(genepop= GenePopData2, nameframe = PopRename, path = paste0(output_dir,&quot;Genepop_grouped_renamed.txt&quot;))
                 
                 "><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>read in the grouped Genepop file</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">GenePopData2</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span>read.table(paste0(<span class="pl-smi">output_dir</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Genepop_grouped.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),<span class="pl-v">header</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">FALSE</span>, <span class="pl-v">sep</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-cce">\t</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-v">quote</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-v">stringsAsFactors</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">FALSE</span>)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>investigate the population parameters</span>
  genepop_detective(<span class="pl-smi">GenePopData2</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Pops<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>we can see that "BBB" &amp; "DDD" and "FFF" &amp; "III" are at the end but still have different names. </span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>create renaming frame</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">PopRename</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> <span class="pl-k">data.frame</span>(<span class="pl-v">oPop</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> c(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>AAA<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>CCC<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>EEE<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>HHH<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>BBB<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>DDD<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>FFF<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>III<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
  <span class="pl-v">newname</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> c(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>AAA<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>CCC<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>EEE<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>HHH<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Group1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Group1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Group2<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Group2<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>Rename the grouped populations</span>
  subset_genepop_rename(<span class="pl-v">genepop</span><span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">GenePopData2</span>, <span class="pl-v">nameframe</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">PopRename</span>, <span class="pl-v">path</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> paste0(<span class="pl-smi">output_dir</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Genepop_grouped_renamed.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))
                 
                 </pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">subset_genepop_individual <a name="user-content-subsetidv"></a></h2><a id="user-content-subset_genepop_individual-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: subset_genepop_individual " href="#subset_genepop_individual-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Remove some individual samples from the dataframe. Here we consider the 'individual' ID to be an alpha-numeric code which at the start of each row of data. The keep parameter defines whether the specified list is removed or retained (default: keep = FALSE).
<em>This function is best run at the beginning of the analysis prior to removal of specific loci or populations.</em> <a href="#funcmanip"><em>Function description</em></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#Use genepop_detective to see the naming structure.
  genepop_detective(GenePopData,&quot;Inds&quot;)

#vector of sample IDs to remove
  subid &lt;- c(&quot;AAA_1&quot;,&quot;AAA_3&quot;,&quot;BBB_20&quot;,&quot;CCC_21&quot;,&quot;EEE_3&quot;,&quot;EEE_26&quot;,&quot;HHH_25&quot;,&quot;JJJ_4&quot;)

  subset_genepop_individual(genepop= GenePopData, indiv = subid, keep = FALSE, path = paste0(output_dir,&quot;Genepop_IDsubset.txt&quot;))"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>Use genepop_detective to see the naming structure.</span>

  <span class="pl-smi">subid</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> c(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>AAA_1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>AAA_3<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>BBB_20<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>CCC_21<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>EEE_3<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>EEE_26<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>HHH_25<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>JJJ_4<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">genepop_reorder <a name="user-content-genepopreorder"></a></h2><a id="user-content-genepop_reorder-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: genepop_reorder " href="#genepop_reorder-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Reorder the genepop file sequentially according to a specified ordering (see below for examples). <a href="#funcmanip"><em>Function description</em></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#Identify populaton names

  genepop_reorder(genepop=&quot;Genepop_IDsubset.txt&quot;,reorder=pops[c(length(pops),2:(length(pops)-1),1)]),path=paste0(output_dir,&quot;GenePop_reordered.txt&quot;)"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>Identify populaton names</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Sampling</strong></h1><a id="user-content-sampling" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Sampling" href="#sampling"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">genepop_sample <a name="user-content-genepopsamp"></a></h2><a id="user-content-genepop_sample-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: genepop_sample " href="#genepop_sample-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Function which will allow you to create subsets of the genepop. This might be useful for creating training and leave-out datasets for assignment. <a href="#funcsamp"><em>Function description</em></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#view how many individuals you have in each population
  genepop_detective(GenePopData,&quot;PopNum&quot;)"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>view how many individuals you have in each population</span>
  genepop_detective(<span class="pl-smi">GenePopData</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>PopNum<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">There are several ways we can sub-sample each population</p>
<p dir="auto">Use a fixed number (e.g. 5 from each population)</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="  SubSamp &lt;- genepop_sample(GenePopData, nsample = 5)"><pre>  <span class="pl-smi">SubSamp</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> genepop_sample(<span class="pl-smi">GenePopData</span>, <span class="pl-v">nsample</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><em>or</em></p>
<p dir="auto">Use a fixed fraction (e.g. 25% from each population)</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="  SubSamp &lt;- genepop_sample(GenePopData, nsample = 0.25)"><pre>  <span class="pl-smi">SubSamp</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> genepop_sample(<span class="pl-smi">GenePopData</span>, <span class="pl-v">nsample</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.25</span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><em>or</em></p>
<p dir="auto">Use a fraction which varies for each population</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#vector of populations in the Genepop file
  Pops &lt;- genepop_detective(GenePopData,&quot;Pops&quot;)

#create a dataframe which defines how many you want to sample from each population. Note here we create a column which has an entry for each population.
  subdf &lt;- data.frame(Pops = Pops, nsample = c(5, 2, 3, 5, 6, 5, 2, 3, 5, 6))

  SubSamp &lt;- genepop_sample(GenePopData, nsample = subdf)"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>vector of populations in the Genepop file</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">Pops</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> genepop_detective(<span class="pl-smi">GenePopData</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Pops<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>create a dataframe which defines how many you want to sample from each population. Note here we create a column which has an entry for each population.</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">subdf</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> <span class="pl-k">data.frame</span>(<span class="pl-v">Pops</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">Pops</span>, <span class="pl-v">nsample</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> c(<span class="pl-c1">5</span>, <span class="pl-c1">2</span>, <span class="pl-c1">3</span>, <span class="pl-c1">5</span>, <span class="pl-c1">6</span>, <span class="pl-c1">5</span>, <span class="pl-c1">2</span>, <span class="pl-c1">3</span>, <span class="pl-c1">5</span>, <span class="pl-c1">6</span>))

  <span class="pl-smi">SubSamp</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> genepop_sample(<span class="pl-smi">GenePopData</span>, <span class="pl-v">nsample</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">subdf</span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><em>or</em></p>
<p dir="auto">Use a fraction which varies for each population</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#vector of populations in the Genepop file
  Pops &lt;- genepop_detective(GenePopData,&quot;Pops&quot;)

#create a dataframe which defines how many you want to sample from each population. Note here we create a column which has an entry for each population.
  subdf &lt;- data.frame(Pops = Pops, nsample = c(5, 2, 3, 5, 6, 5, 2, 3, 5, 6)/10)

  SubSamp &lt;- genepop_sample(GenePopData, nsample = subdf)"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>vector of populations in the Genepop file</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">Pops</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> genepop_detective(<span class="pl-smi">GenePopData</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Pops<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>create a dataframe which defines how many you want to sample from each population. Note here we create a column which has an entry for each population.</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">subdf</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> <span class="pl-k">data.frame</span>(<span class="pl-v">Pops</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">Pops</span>, <span class="pl-v">nsample</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> c(<span class="pl-c1">5</span>, <span class="pl-c1">2</span>, <span class="pl-c1">3</span>, <span class="pl-c1">5</span>, <span class="pl-c1">6</span>, <span class="pl-c1">5</span>, <span class="pl-c1">2</span>, <span class="pl-c1">3</span>, <span class="pl-c1">5</span>, <span class="pl-c1">6</span>)<span class="pl-k">/</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span>)

  <span class="pl-smi">SubSamp</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> genepop_sample(<span class="pl-smi">GenePopData</span>, <span class="pl-v">nsample</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">subdf</span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Once you select a method to sub-sample each population, you can use the function subset-genepop-indiv to create the sampled genepop file.</p>
<p dir="auto">For example if you wanted to create a training and assignment dataset  in genepop format using the random stratified sampled we selected using subset-genepop-indiv:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#Create training dataset (keep = TRUE)
  subset_genepop_individual(GenePopData, indiv = SubSamp, keep = TRUE, path = paste0(output_dir,&quot;Genepop_training.txt&quot;))

#Create an assignment dataset using the remaining individuals (keep = FALSE)
  subset_genepop_individual(GenePopData, indiv = SubSamp, keep = FALSE, path = paste0(output_dir,&quot;Genepop_assignment.txt&quot;))"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>Create training dataset (keep = TRUE)</span>
  subset_genepop_individual(<span class="pl-smi">GenePopData</span>, <span class="pl-v">indiv</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">SubSamp</span>, <span class="pl-v">keep</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">TRUE</span>, <span class="pl-v">path</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> paste0(<span class="pl-smi">output_dir</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Genepop_training.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>Create an assignment dataset using the remaining individuals (keep = FALSE)</span>
  subset_genepop_individual(<span class="pl-smi">GenePopData</span>, <span class="pl-v">indiv</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">SubSamp</span>, <span class="pl-v">keep</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">FALSE</span>, <span class="pl-v">path</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> paste0(<span class="pl-smi">output_dir</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Genepop_assignment.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))</pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Conversion</strong></h1><a id="user-content-conversion" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Conversion" href="#conversion"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">genepop_structure <a name="user-content-genepopstruc"></a></h2><a id="user-content-genepop_structure-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: genepop_structure " href="#genepop_structure-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If you are interested in investigating population structure you can convert your modified Genepop object or path to saved file directly into a <a href="http://web.stanford.edu/group/pritchardlab/structure.html" rel="nofollow">STRUCTURE</a> formatted text (.str) file &lt;&gt;. <a href="#funcconvert"><em>Function description</em></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#convert Genepop format to STRUCTURE to default groupings
  genepop_structure(genepop=&quot;Genepop_IDsubset.txt&quot;,path = paste0(output_dir,&quot;Sturcture_IDsubset_groups.txt&quot;))
  
# Specify population groupings (group CCC/DDD/EEE and III/JJJ)
  pGroups &lt;- data.frame(pops = c(&quot;AAA&quot;,&quot;BBB&quot;,&quot;CCC&quot;,&quot;DDD&quot;,&quot;EEE&quot;,&quot;FFF&quot;,&quot;GGG&quot;,&quot;HHH&quot;,&quot;III&quot;,&quot;JJJ&quot;),groups = c(&quot;1&quot;,&quot;2&quot;,&quot;3&quot;,&quot;3&quot;,&quot;3&quot;,&quot;4&quot;,&quot;5&quot;,&quot;6&quot;,&quot;7&quot;,&quot;7&quot;))

#convert Genepop format to STRUCTURE with new groupings
  genepop_structure(genepop=&quot;Genepop_IDsubset.txt&quot;,popgroup = pGroups, path = paste0(output_dir,&quot;Sturcture_IDsubset_groups.txt&quot;))
"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>convert Genepop format to STRUCTURE to default groupings</span>
  genepop_structure(<span class="pl-v">genepop</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Genepop_IDsubset.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-v">path</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> paste0(<span class="pl-smi">output_dir</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Sturcture_IDsubset_groups.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))
  
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Specify population groupings (group CCC/DDD/EEE and III/JJJ)</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">pGroups</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> <span class="pl-k">data.frame</span>(<span class="pl-v">pops</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> c(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>AAA<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>BBB<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>CCC<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>DDD<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>EEE<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>FFF<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>GGG<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>HHH<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>III<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>JJJ<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),<span class="pl-v">groups</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> c(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>2<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>3<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>3<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>3<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>4<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>5<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>6<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>7<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>7<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>convert Genepop format to STRUCTURE with new groupings</span>
  genepop_structure(<span class="pl-v">genepop</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Genepop_IDsubset.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-v">popgroup</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">pGroups</span>, <span class="pl-v">path</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> paste0(<span class="pl-smi">output_dir</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Sturcture_IDsubset_groups.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))
</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">genepop_fstat <a name="user-content-genepopfst"></a></h2><a id="user-content-genepop_fstat-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: genepop_fstat " href="#genepop_fstat-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If you are interested in doing calculating gene diversities and-or F-statistics with the cleaned loci datasets, you can convert from Genepop to FSTAT format
This data can be used by the R package <a href="https://cran.r-project.org/web/packages/hierfstat/index.html" rel="nofollow">hierfstat</a> or the program <a href="http://www2.unil.ch/popgen/softwares/fstat.htm" rel="nofollow">FSTAT</a> <a href="#funcconvert"><em>Function description</em></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#convert Genepop format to FSTAT (.dat)
  genepop_fstat(genepop=&quot;Genepop_IDsubset.txt&quot;,path = paste0(output_dir,&quot;Fstat_IDsubset.dat&quot;))

#convert Genepop format to FSTAT but keep the data in the workspace
  genepop_fstat(genepop=&quot;Genepop_IDsubset.txt&quot;,addworkspace = TRUE)"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>convert Genepop format to FSTAT (.dat)</span>
  genepop_fstat(<span class="pl-v">genepop</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Genepop_IDsubset.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-v">path</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> paste0(<span class="pl-smi">output_dir</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Fstat_IDsubset.dat<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>convert Genepop format to FSTAT but keep the data in the workspace</span>
  genepop_fstat(<span class="pl-v">genepop</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Genepop_IDsubset.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-v">addworkspace</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">TRUE</span>)</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">genepop_newhybrids <a name="user-content-genepopnh"></a></h2><a id="user-content-genepop_newhybrids-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: genepop_newhybrids " href="#genepop_newhybrids-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If you are interested in testing for hybridization you can convert from Genepop to the format necessary for the program <a href="http://ib.berkeley.edu/labs/slatkin/eriq/software/software.htm#NewHybs" rel="nofollow">New Hybrids</a> <a href="#funcconvert"><em>Function description</em></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#convert Genepop format to New Hybrids format (.txt)
  genepop_newhybrids(genepop=&quot;Genepop_IDsubset.txt&quot;,path = paste0(output_dir,&quot;NewHybrids_IDsubset.txt&quot;))"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>convert Genepop format to New Hybrids format (.txt)</span>
  genepop_newhybrids(<span class="pl-v">genepop</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Genepop_IDsubset.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-v">path</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> paste0(<span class="pl-smi">output_dir</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>NewHybrids_IDsubset.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">genepop_assigner <a name="user-content-genepopagn"></a></h2><a id="user-content-genepop_assigner-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: genepop_assigner " href="#genepop_assigner-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If you are interested conducting assignment analysis, you can convert to the format required for the R package <a href="https://github.com/thierrygosselin/assigner">assigner</a> <a href="#funcconvert"><em>Function description</em></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#convert Genepop format to assigner format (.txt) using the populations each as their own assessment level
  genepop_assigner(genepop=&quot;Genepop_IDsubset.txt&quot;,path = paste0(output_dir,&quot;assigner_IDsubset.txt&quot;))
  
# Set new population assignment groupings (group CCC/DDD/EEE and III/JJJ)
  pGroups &lt;- data.frame(pops = c(&quot;AAA&quot;,&quot;BBB&quot;,&quot;CCC&quot;,&quot;DDD&quot;,&quot;EEE&quot;,&quot;FFF&quot;,&quot;GGG&quot;,&quot;HHH&quot;,&quot;III&quot;,&quot;JJJ&quot;),groups = c(&quot;1&quot;,&quot;2&quot;,&quot;3&quot;,&quot;3&quot;,&quot;3&quot;,&quot;4&quot;,&quot;5&quot;,&quot;6&quot;,&quot;7&quot;,&quot;7&quot;))
   
   genepop_assigner(genepop=&quot;Genepop_IDsubset.txt&quot;,popgroup = pGroups, path = paste0(output_dir,&quot;assigner_IDsubset_NewGroups.txt&quot;))
  "><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>convert Genepop format to assigner format (.txt) using the populations each as their own assessment level</span>
  genepop_assigner(<span class="pl-v">genepop</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Genepop_IDsubset.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-v">path</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> paste0(<span class="pl-smi">output_dir</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>assigner_IDsubset.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))
  
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Set new population assignment groupings (group CCC/DDD/EEE and III/JJJ)</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">pGroups</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> <span class="pl-k">data.frame</span>(<span class="pl-v">pops</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> c(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>AAA<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>BBB<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>CCC<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>DDD<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>EEE<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>FFF<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>GGG<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>HHH<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>III<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>JJJ<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),<span class="pl-v">groups</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> c(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>2<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>3<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>3<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>3<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>4<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>5<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>6<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>7<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>7<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))
   
   genepop_assigner(<span class="pl-v">genepop</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Genepop_IDsubset.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-v">popgroup</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">pGroups</span>, <span class="pl-v">path</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> paste0(<span class="pl-smi">output_dir</span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>assigner_IDsubset_NewGroups.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">genepop_colony <a name="user-content-genepopcolony"></a></h2><a id="user-content-genepop_colony-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: genepop_colony " href="#genepop_colony-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If you are interested in investigating sibship or parentage, you can convert to the format required for the software <a href="https://www.zsl.org/science/software/colony" rel="nofollow">Colony</a>. Returned are functions for translating the Colony output and those required by the maximum likelihood analysis. 'Individual' and 'Loci' conversion files can be used to match the loci and individual names formatted for input to Colony to those provided as input by the user.'MarkerTypeErrorRT' file defines the allele dropout rates as calculated using the 'missing' function in PLINK. Rates of other error types are assumed to be equal to the estimated allele dropout rates. 'GENOTYPES' are the geneotypes in two columns per loci format. Output from Colony is based on the input for of the
'GENOTYPES' file. Original loci and individual names can be assigned using the conversion output files. All files are returned to path and are named according tot he input filename. <a href="#funcconvert"><em>Function description</em></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#convert Genepop format to the files necessary for Colony 
  genepop_colony(genepop=&quot;Genepop_IDsubset.txt&quot;,where.plink=&quot;c:/Users/YOURNAME/Documents/Programs/plink/&quot;,where.pgdspider=&quot;c:/Users/YOURNAME/Documents/Programs/PGDSpider_2.0.9.0/&quot;,denote.missing = &quot;000&quot;,path = output_dir)
  "><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>convert Genepop format to the files necessary for Colony </span>
  genepop_colony(<span class="pl-v">genepop</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Genepop_IDsubset.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-v">where.plink</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>c:/Users/YOURNAME/Documents/Programs/plink/<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-v">where.pgdspider</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>c:/Users/YOURNAME/Documents/Programs/PGDSpider_2.0.9.0/<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-v">denote.missing</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>000<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-v">path</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">output_dir</span>)
  </pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">genepop_bgc <a name="user-content-genepopbgc"></a></h2><a id="user-content-genepop_bgc-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: genepop_bgc " href="#genepop_bgc-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>genepopedit</strong> is one of the few tools available to convert data to the format required for input into to the <a href="https://sites.google.com/site/bgcsoftware/" rel="nofollow">Bayesian estimation of Genomic Clines</a> (BGC) format. BGC can evalute genomic clinal patterns and introgression among loci. To convert to BGC format you must specify which populations you consider to be ancestral or <strong>parental</strong> (P1, P2) and which you assume could be hybridized (<strong>admixed</strong>). <a href="#funcconvert"><em>Function description</em></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#specify which populations are going to be included in the analysis and to which class they belong. Note Pops identified in P1 and-or P2 can also be specified as &quot;Admixed&quot; to test BGC output. 
  BGC_groups = data.frame(pops = c(&quot;AAA&quot;,&quot;BBB&quot;,&quot;CCC&quot;,&quot;DDD&quot;,&quot;EEE&quot;,&quot;FFF&quot;,&quot;GGG&quot;,&quot;HHH&quot;,&quot;III&quot;,&quot;JJJ&quot;),groups = c(&quot;P1&quot;,&quot;P1&quot;,&quot;P1&quot;,&quot;Admixed&quot;,&quot;Admixed&quot;,&quot;Admixed&quot;,&quot;Admixed&quot;,&quot;P2&quot;,&quot;P2&quot;,&quot;P2&quot;))

#convert Genepop to BGC input files (3). Note in this case the variable path is a path to the directory where the input files will be saved.
  genepop_bgc(genepop=&quot;Genepop_IDsubset.txt&quot;,popdef = BGC_groups, fname=&quot;BGC_IDsubset&quot;,path = output_dir)
"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>specify which populations are going to be included in the analysis and to which class they belong. Note Pops identified in P1 and-or P2 can also be specified as "Admixed" to test BGC output. </span>
  <span class="pl-v">BGC_groups</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">data.frame</span>(<span class="pl-v">pops</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> c(<span class="pl-s"><span
